In a fast-paced 2D action game, holding a button for 3 full seconds feels like an eternity and might cause players to think the game is broken.\n> **Recommendation:** I strongly recommend using **1 second (1000ms)** or even **0.5 seconds (500ms)** for the long press. My plan below uses 1000ms, but if you strictly want 3000ms, let me know!\n\n> [!IMPORTANT]\n> **Action on Release:** Because a short press of A harvests the block, the game must wait to see if you are holding the button. This means short actions (harvesting/deploying) will trigger exactly when you **release** the A button (if held for less than 1s). The long press combo will trigger automatically while holding the button down after 1s has passed.\n\n## Proposed Changes\n\n### `player.ts`\n\n- **Remove Menu Binding:** Delete `controller.menu.onEvent`.\n- **Restore B Button:** Revert `controller.B.onEvent` to toggle the inventory (`!inventoryOpen = true`).\n- **Implement Long/Short Press State:**\n  - Add globals `let aPressStart = 0` and `let aLongPressTriggered = false`.\n  - On `controller.A.onEvent(ControllerButtonEvent.Pressed)`: Record `aPressStart = game.runtime()` and set triggered to false.\n  - On `controller.A.onEvent(ControllerButtonEvent.Released)`: If duration is under 1000ms, call `performShortAction()`. Reset `aPressStart`.\n  - In `game.onUpdate()`: If A is being held and duration > 1000ms, call `performLongAction()`.\n- **Function: `performShortAction()`:**\n  - Only executes Harvesing OR Deploying.\n  - If `isHarvestable(frontId)`, it harvests it immediately.\n  - Otherwise, if `matCount() > 0`, it deploys the resource on an empty square (`GRASS`, `WATER`, `DUNGEON_FLOOR`).\n- **Function: `performLongAction()`:**\n  - Only checks for Combinable Types.\n  - Implements the new symmetric rules:\n    - **Fire:** Target `HAY` + Selected `WOOD` **OR** Target `TIMBER` + Selected `HAY`\n    - **Scarecrow:** Target `HAY` + Selected `SPIKES` **OR** Target `SPIKES` + Selected `HAY`\n  - Fueling an existing Campfire will also be handled here.\n\n## Verification Plan\n\n1. Test opening the inventory with `B`.\n2. Select Spikes. Tap `A` facing an empty square -> deploys Spikes.\n3. Tap `A` facing Spikes -> harvests Spikes.\n4. Select Hay. Tap `A` facing an empty square -> deploys Hay.\n5. With Hay selected, look at Spikes and hold `A` for 1 second -> Spikes transform into a Scarecrow.\n6. Test Wood + Hay combinations for Fire.\n\n"}

Context-Sensitive `A` Button\n\nThe `A` button has been split into two distinct actions based on how long you hold it down:\n\n**Short Press (< 1000ms)**\nExecutes instantly upon *releasing* the `A` button.\n* **Harvesting**: Releasing `A` on a valid resource (e.g., Trees, Ores, or placed structures) will harvest it.\n* **Deploying**: If looking at empty space (Grass/Water) with a resource selected, releasing `A` deploys it.\n\n**Long Press (>= 1000ms)**\nExecutes automatically once you have held the `A` button down for a full second.\n* **Combinations**: If you are looking at a block that can be combined with your currently selected item, holding `A` will consume your item and transform the target block. If no combination is valid, holding `A` does nothing.\n\n### 3. Symmetrical Combo Building\n\nThe long press action checks for the following perfectly symmetrical combinations:\n* **Campfire**:\n  * Looking at `HAY` with `WOOD` selected.\n  * Looking at `TIMBER` with `HAY` selected.\n* **Scarecrow**:\n  * Looking at `HAY` with `SPIKES` selected.\n  * Looking at `SPIKES` with `HAY` selected.\n* **Campfire Fueling**: Holding a long press with either Wood or Hay selected while looking at an existing Campfire will fuel it.\n\n> [!TIP]\n> The Long Press timer was set to 1000ms (1 second) to ensure the game remains snappy. 0.5 seconds is extremely long for real-time actions, but if you'd like to increase the threshold, it only takes a single line change!\n\n## Verification\n\n* The project compiles perfectly without any TypeScript errors.\n* `PROJECT_STATE.md` has been updated with these new mechanics.\n* You can test the interaction immediately in your local emulator!\n\n## Controls Rework: Long Press Fix\n\nI have implemented the long press functionality as requested using `controller.setRepeatDefault()` and counting `ControllerButtonEvent.Repeated` triggers. A press of under 0.5 seconds will fire `performShortAction` (harvest/build) upon release, and holding it for 0.5 seconds will trigger `performLongAction` (combinations/scarecrow/fire).\n\n"}
